North Bridge  Intel Comet Lake-S IMC

Tecnologia utilizada  14 nm
VT-d  Suportado
Extended APIC (x2APIC)  Suportado
 
Controlador de memória:
Tipo  Dual Channel (128 bits)
Modo Ativo  Dual Channel (128 bits)
 
Temporização de Memória:
CAS Latency (CL)  17T
RAS To CAS Delay (tRCD)  17T
RAS Precharge (tRP)  17T
RAS Active Time (tRAS)  39T
Row Refresh Cycle Time (tRFC)  421T
Command Rate (CR)  2T
RAS To RAS Delay (tRRD)  Same Bank Group: 6T, Diff. Bank Group: 4T
Write Recovery Time (tWR)  19T
Read To Read Delay (tRTR)  Different Rank: 7T, Different DIMM: 8T, Same Bank Group: 6T, Diff. Bank Group: 4T
